		"information_description1"						"<h1>At the start of the game, you need to set up an unfinished tent just outside the base of troll and run to your desired base, let your allies know in advance on which base you are going by pinging it beforehand. After you arrived to the base, put one stone on the entrance, set up an awning and immediately upgrade it. Be sure to put a flag near the stone, it increases the damage received by the troll by 50%, magical damage by 35% and reduces outgoing damage from the troll by 10% in a radius of 900.
P.S. to send the flag to your friend, you need to open the score table
and click flag next to your friend's nickname.
P.S. Pick a base as far away from the troll's base as possible."
		"information_description2"						"<h1>At the beginning of the game, if the troll comes to you, No need to panic! You should give the troll a root (located in your inventory) so that the troll can't attack or move. After the root effect ends, give Glyph (item) to your wall (during the duration of the glyph, the troll does not deal damage to the wall and denies him of any farm).
I also advise you not to build towers until you have upgraded tent2 to tent3 and in no case do not immediately upgrade the towers to lvl2, because it is cheaper to first put a lot of lvl 1 towers and only then you can upgrade it to lvl 2 later."
		"information_description3"						"<h1>If you see that you can’t keep up on repairing the wall by yourself, then you need to build workers/repairers from the workers guild and send them to repair the wall"
